<review>I have not been here yet to buy my trike, however this was on my mind as I scrolled through the reviews....

Ive seen posts about the prices being high. Perhaps prices are set by cost of living? Its costs a small fortune just to get started in business here in Apple Valley. Permits ,inspections etc. I know, because I have just paid all those fees to get started here. I have spent at least $400 getting business licenses and inspections and office-permits. In Riverside county Canyon Lake Calif. no inspections for $300, no office permit for $150. Just a biz license for $100 . And renewal is $41 per year. Blah blah blah.

So those who can get it cheaper elsewhere, is probably because cost of living and doing business in your home town is less costly.  Just me sticking up for small business owner!,</review>< name>

< text>
Manager and some of the staff are often rude, offensive, and disrespectful. The "do not disturb" sign is meaningless to house keeping and maintenance, they will ignore it and knock anyway. Bugs kept getting in room and staff suggested I not open the door as a solution. Don't be surprised if and when you hear, feel, and perhaps even see people having sex. If that's not something you want to experience, tough, nothing will be done. The extremely positive reviews are probably those very people, the ones who are not bothered are often times the ones doing the bothering. Most front desk employees and managers, with the exception of the very sweet girl who works in the morning/day are extremely unhelpful. Deluxe room was wonderful, however. It was spacious, clean, flat screen tv, comfortable bed, microwave, fridge, brand new furniture, hair dryer, all for a good price. The rooms aren't the issue, its a couple of the employees and some of the disrespectful, selfish, and inconsiderate guests that are a huge problem and why I left. And not to mention, why I will not be returning.</text>

<Review>This is a Nice Speakeasy. I've been to about 6 different Speakeasy's and this one is ranked somewhere above average. The entrance is a bit disappointing because it isn't hidden and it just takes away from the mystique of a hidden bar.... although the Vault Door is very cool.
Now, where this place really shine's is it's customer service. They are very friendly and the best part is they are very organized. If your reservation is at 10pm, they are ready for you at 10pm....Big A+.  The drinks are very well made. Bartender's take there time to make your drink correctly. Also the decor is on point. <text>Lovely little coffee shop in Scott's Valley with delicious coffee, delightful pastries, and friendly baristas. They knew their regulars well, which is always a good sign. They had a lot of food too, not just coffee. They serve Lulu Carpenter's coffee here, which I had never had before, and their espresso was very nice, bright, bold, with a hint of berry (to my taste buds at least).

My wife loved her latte with whole milk, which she usually sweetens but didn't and still really enjoyed. Her breakfast bagel was also very good. My cappuccino was bright, the espresso strong, and the oat milk (Oatly Barista) paired well with it. I also ate a Lemon poppyseed with lemon curd muffin which was really nice and moist. Such a lovely way to start the day.

Highly recommend checking it out. Plenty of outdoor seating too. <Response>None</Response><Review>I Love Coffee!!

So driving to Santa Cruz and had a craving for coffee so yelped this place and seemed like great reviews. Decided to check it out. Parking out side was a breeze. Plenty of parking available. Walking in the store has a nice coffee smell. Everything in the shop looks clean and professional and organized. Felt like a homey coffee shop.

There was a group of 7 of us and we all got our own special coffee. For the 7 of us the barista did a very fast and accurate job and even made foam prints on our lattes (unfortunately forgot to take a picture). I personally got the coconut syrup hot latte and my fianc茅 got the same thing but iced. The quality of the drink was acceptable.

1 small downside.  Not sure if they don't provide it or if they just didn't have any when we were there but they didn't have any hot cup sleeves. When I asked she kindly offered a second cup which was nice.

Coffee Cat is part of Lulu Carpenter's, a long-standing local company which has several cafes in Santa Cruz. In my experience they have been making excellent coffee for decades. If you're headed in or out of Santa Cruz and want good coffee off of Highway 17 check out Coffee Cat.</Text>< Pics>

< Review>
I sadly misjudged Coffee Cat for many months and titled my nose as I drove past to visit Starbucks and Peet's for my regular coffee & work sessions. But thankfully the coffee gods did not give up on me and recently guided my vehicle to Coffee Cat.

Boy have I been missing out! Upon walking in I was excited to see a very spacious seating area with nice wood tables and way less people than the other big-name coffee shops. They even have power outlets along the entire wall for all those seated along it - amazing! The wifi is also very good and the bathrooms are decently clean.

And to my even greater surprise, they have a Clover!! I love coffee pulled from a Clover, always my first choice if available which is rare. Their other coffee selections are also very good and the ladies really know what they are doing behind the counter. They also have a great food selection with healthy, authentic ingredients. And if that isn't enough, Safeway is right next door - very convenient.

Overall, I am very impressed with Coffee Cat and have directed all of my coffee funds and work sessions here. Thank you CC!< /Review>

<Time>1560902264351<//Time>< Review>
I tried to be happy with the results since my car IS cleaner, but this has been eating at me since yesterday afternoon. I've come here for years and yesterday was the first and last time I ever come here for a detailing. It's also the first time I haven't tipped.

$170 for a full detail and seat/carpet shampoo. Three hours. After all that money and time, they missed: bug goo on the hood, the driver's side and passenger side sun visors, gear shift, sides of center console, dust in the vent slats, and still some dust remaining in crevices. My car also smelled vaguely of wet dirt afterwards.

I get that cleaning cars is exhausting. I paid the price to have the job done better than I could do it. Unfortunately that expectation wasn't met and now I have to follow-up on my off day. I could do better in 5-6 hours what they did with multiple people in 3.

This place is great for a quick wash and vacuum, but you should probably go to a specialty company for detailing.

Update: The fabric panelling on the driver's side door has started to bubble up. That's it, I'm going to ask for a refund. Not only is this a job badly done but now my car is damaged. Thanks.

Update 2: I asked for a refund yesterday and they said all they could do is detail my car again. They might think I'm a pushover because I try so hard to be nice, even when stuff like this happens. Really it's just that I don't have the time to bother with it and don't want them touching my car after they damaged it. I could technically file an insurance claim but again, won't bother. I'll be contacting my bank for a refund instead. I'm also pleased that my review brought their rating from 4.0 to 3.9. Never coming back here, they should call themselves "Whatever Wheel Car Wash" because that's the level of service you get here.

Update 3: I got a full refund through Wells Fargo, although it took 30 days because Water Wheel didn't respond to the transaction dispute.

Thanks for reading!< /Review>

My daughter's Honda was overheating and I live 3,000 miles away from Corona. I found MVT by calling NAPA and asking the counter guy "where is the best repair shop in town?" They told me that this place does all kinds of repairs (not just tires) and that they were good. I called their manager, Charles, and from the get-go, he was really good. They checked my daughter's compression and found the head gasket was blown. He said that they sub out their motor rebuilds and that their shop had done hundreds of jobs for them with only 1 issue, a transmission that was replaced after it failed.
Long story short: the Honda engine was rebuilt for exactly what they said it would cost. I was in constant contact with Mountain View, who kept tabs on the rebuild shop for me and they never even charged me for the engine check! The car runs great and I don't have to worry about my kid. Thank you Charles, I'm sure my daughter will be back if she has any other problems (engine was warrantied for 6 years, so I'll bet it won't be for that!)

I think the key is to get there EARLY, and have all your paperwork ready. Nobody wants to go to the DMV, but it sure is a popular place. Good luck! </Text>

<Time>1598675563503</Time><review>After having read the reviews, I was expecting the worse...

First, do not trust the waiting time estimates on their website. Without any appointment (which you can't book at this time), you will have to queue for 3 to 4 hours. Do not come in the afternoon, there is little chance you will get in.

I agree that, especially with this pandemic, they should control the crowds by doing appointment only instead of having people standing in line in the heat for hours. The DMV managers should rethink their system, for sure.

Having said that, I arrived at 6AM to start queuing, there were already 50 people or so. I got in at 9AM, passed the written test, booked a behind-the-wheel test directly after, and got my driver license in the afternoon. I don't know of any other country where you could get your driver license in a day.

Everyone at the DMV was nice and helpful, patient and arranging. I understand that people get angry when they get told to go at the end of the line to do simple administrative tasks, but it's not the employees fault. <Gmap_id>0x80dce87e8cfd0a97:0xc47c2586563974a8<//Gmap_id>< text>
I was joking with the guy in line next to me that all DMVs have less than stellar ratings but after my experience today I thought I'd leave a rating of my mostly positive experience. First, 5 stars for Christine (Christina?), the lady at door. Her kindness made my day.  I wanted to thank her on the way out but she was helping another customer. The whole process took about 2.5 hrs, which is long, but I had low expectations going into the situation. I needed to renew my ID including a name change as well as submit Real ID paperwork. I filled out the forms online and was able to make an appointment. Unfortunately, the appointment was a few weeks after my due date and I did not want to bring a newborn to the DMV. So, I decided to brave the lines and wait. It took maybe an hour to get in, an hour to get served, and 30 minutes at the window. I took off one star because the guy at my window was really unprepared. He couldn't find the key to the cash drawer then he didn't have change. He had taken over for someone that had gone on a break and didn't seem quite ready to start processing paperwork. REMEMBER: cash, check, or debit only. I recommend exact change. The sound system is sort of broken, so windows one and twenty one often read as "one" over the loud speaker. Consequently, several people kept coming over to window one while I was being served, interrupting the guy helping me out. The DMV in general could use an update of its computer system.

Tips for DMV survival:
Fill out forms online
Have your documents accessible and ready.
Be prepared to wait. Everyone else has somewhere to be too.
Be kind. I heard people asking the same questions over and over. Don't take out your anger on the employees because you didn't read what was required ahead of time.
Appointments: Meh, you have to wait in line outside regardless. You'll get served faster once you're in but you still have to wait. Appointments aren't a fast pass. You've been warned.
The DMV needs a revamp from the top down. I couldn't make an appointment without filling out the online forms first but that wasn't posted anywhere. The next appointment was nearly 3 months out. The workers at the window are working with the same system. It just sucks.
Bring a book or some kind of entertainment.< /text>

< review>
I dreaded and put off going to the DMV to get a Real ID for almost a year because of everyone's incredibly negative reviews. Personally, my experience was great! I went on a Friday afternoon at 1:15pm and was out at 3:00pm. I had to wait in line a bit and then once I got my first ticket # I had to sit waiting ~40mins longer, take the written test, photo, etc., and all 5 DMV workers I interacted with were great. They were friendly, helped clarify any questions, and did their jobs efficiently.

This is a DMV. You know you have to wait in line. You know it won't be a fun afternoon. No DMV is going to be a perfect experience filled with unicorns and sunshine, so I really don't understand why so many people leave a terrible review for the exact thing they know they're walking into? Maybe I just got lucky, but I don't think it is a coincidence that every person/station I interacted with was great. I would give this DMV a shot! Don't listen to the 2/5 star reviews!</review>

Best SoCal DMV I've ever been to. I've been there a dozen times for various things over the last 3 years. This last time really impressed me - I went in to get a new RealID DL, and I was in and out in less than 30 minutes. < Review>
I could not see any available appointments online so decided to do the usual show up well early for less wait. I arrived at 6.40am and only had 10-15 people in front of me. At 7.30am, the Starbucks next door came around too give everyone little samples of coffee and donuts. At 7.45am, the staff started organizing us between people here for driving licence and registrations. Those of us here for DL matter were let into the building and given directions to make things go faster once the windows were open. My recommendation: do the online application ahead of time. I went from 15th in line to 3rd in line! It was a long wait before opening but things are run smoothly once it opens.

I also got to experience great customer service. Still half asleep when I left, I absentmindedly forgot ALL MY DOCUMENTS on the bench when my ride arrived.  I only realized later than evening (its was Friday) and was worried all weekend. I received a piece of mail on Monday from the DMV with one of my documents and a little notes that said to come pick up the rest. Showed up, showed some ID and got all my documents back!<//Review>

< text>
We went to the Laguna DMV today for New CA Resident Real IDs for 2 people and VIN Verification and Car Registration. We arrived at 8:30 am WITHOUT AN APPOINTMENT and it took about 5 hours WHICH INCLUDED 2 trips back home to get the correct documents for myself (both times my fault), and my husband leaving again to get a SMOG check and another time the computer system went down for a moment and restarted the systems. Had we had all the paperwork needed for the IDs and SMOG check completed, I believe we would have been out of there in less than 3 hours. Which I think is great for 4 out of state items. Each time I had to leave, I was asked to return to a special line "between the orange flags" and did not have to re-wait in the long lines.

Everyone that I encountered was pleasant. I want to give a shout out to ***Ms. TERRI *** She was very patient with me and greeted me with a smile every time I had to leave and come back with more information.

TIPS FOR VISITORS
1. Arrive Early!!!
When I arrived at 8:30am/Monday there were 3 employees working at the check-in desk and one person in front of me. When I left and came back at 9am-ish, 2 of the employees had been pulled away from the desk and reassigned to other stations leaving only 1 employee at the check-in desk for many hours. By 12pm the line was OUT THE DOOR and up the walk way!!!

2. Eat something before you arrive and/or bring clean eating snacks.
You are going to have to wait. It is just how it is and getting the "hangries" is not going to make the experience anymore pleasant and will not make the visit go by faster.

3. Be careful how much you drink and bring Poopouri Spray
There is only 1 toilet in the Lady's Room (I do not know about the Men's Room). The line can get long and the room can get unpleasant.

4. Read over the California Driver's Handbook while you wait
SURPRISE!!! There is a Q&A drivers test as part of the application process.<//text>

As I assumed,  my trip to the DMV would be a process (lets be honest,  it always is).  I usually go to the san clemente DMV, but it's closed for renovations.

Laguna was as good as it gets for a DMV.

I got there 10 minutes early (i suggest going earlier).  I overheard that if you want to take a behind the wheel test, you need to make an appointment a few weeks in advance.

anyway,  there were two employees going down the line helping answer questions and directing people.  This meant once we got in,  we were good to go.

I got my number.

sat down.

Then the entire California DMV system went down.

Were people upset?  sure.  But it's not the employees fault.  The problem was in Sacramento.

The bottom line is that all employees here were very VERY communicative and constantly let us know what was going on.

The system turned back on,  I handled my errands,  and I was out.

Granted the DMV isn't ever an experience we look forward to,  but the employees here made it as painless as possible.</review>
